     <div class="afd-post-stream clearfix " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">
      <div class="custom-tag-streamlogo">
      </div>
      <h3 class="afd-title-big afd-title-big--bmargin-small afd-mobile-margin">
       <a class="afd-title--black-link" href="/cn/769023/jiao-dian-pi-ai-er-star-nai-er-wei">
        <span itemprop="name">
         聚焦：皮埃尔·奈尔维
        </span>
       </a>
      </h3>
      <div class="date-publication afd-mobile-margin">
       <meta content="2018-06-21" itemprop="datePublished"/>
       16:30 - 21 六月, 2018
      </div>
      <div class="afd-post-content " itemprop="articleBody">
       <figure aria-labelledby="figcaption_newsroom-picture-att-id-557fbf05e58ece71030000c2" class="js-image-size media-picture" data-height="424" data-width="640" id="newsroom-picture-att-id-557fbf05e58ece71030000c2" style="width: 640px; height: 424px;">
        <a class="js-image-size__link lazy-anchor" href="/cn/769023/jiao-dian-pi-ai-er-star-nai-er-wei" rel="attachment" style="width: 640px; height: 424px;">
         <img alt="聚焦：皮埃尔·奈尔维, Palazzetto dello sport. Image © &lt;a href='https://www.flickr.com/photos/ihavegotthestyle/221174130'&gt;Flickr user ihavegotthestyle&lt;/a&gt; licensed under &lt;a href='https://creativecommons.org/licenses/by/2.0/'&gt;CC BY 2.0&lt;/a&gt;" class="b-lazy" data-nr-picture-id="557fbf05e58ece71030000c2" data-src="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/557f/bf05/e58e/ce71/0300/00c2/newsletter/221174130_921ee9be84_o.jpg?1434435318" data-src-small="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/557f/bf05/e58e/ce71/0300/00c2/medium_jpg/221174130_921ee9be84_o.jpg?1434435318" itemprop="image" longdesc="https://www.archdaily.cn/cn/769023/jiao-dian-pi-ai-er-star-nai-er-wei/557fbf05e58ece71030000c2-spotlight-pier-luigi-nervi-2-photo" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAUEBAAAACwAAAAAAQABAAACAkQBADs="/>
        </a>
        <figcaption class="figcaption afd-desktop-e" id="figcaption_newsroom-picture-att-id-557fbf05e58ece71030000c2">
         Palazzetto dello sport. Image ©
         <a class="sanitized-link" href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/ihavegotthestyle/221174130" target="_blank">
          Flickr user ihavegotthestyle
         </a>
         licensed under
         <a class="sanitized-link" href="https://creativecommons.org/licenses/by/2.0/" target="_blank">
          CC BY 2.0
         </a>
        </figcaption>
        <i class="figcaption-cc-icon afd-desktop-e">
        </i>
       </figure>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
        作为一位公认的建筑师和工程师，皮埃尔·奈尔维
        <a href="http://www.archdaily.com/tag/pier-luigi-nervi/" target="_blank">
         Pier Luigi Nervi
        </a>
        (1891.6.21-1979.1.9)通过创造一系列创新的结构醒深入探索了钢筋混凝土的极限；在这个过程中，他促使混凝土在随后几年到来的建筑运动中占有一席之地。奈尔维在科技革命时代开始他的职业生涯，基于他的抱负和在挑战中发现机遇的能力，他对一些学科和文化产生了影响。
       </p>
      </div>
      <div class="hidden">
       <span itemprop="url">
        https://www.archdaily.cn/cn/769023/jiao-dian-pi-ai-er-star-nai-er-wei
       </span>
       <span itemprop="author" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        Patrick Kunkel
       </span>
      </div>

     <div class="afd-post-stream clearfix " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">
      <div class="custom-tag-streamlogo">
      </div>
      <h3 class="afd-title-big afd-title-big--bmargin-small afd-mobile-margin">
       <a class="afd-title--black-link" href="/cn/896688/na-zuo-cheng-shi-yong-you-zui-duo-gao-ceng-jian-zhu">
        <span itemprop="name">
         哪座城市拥有最多高层建筑？
        </span>
       </a>
      </h3>
      <div class="date-publication afd-mobile-margin">
       <meta content="2018-06-21" itemprop="datePublished"/>
       13:30 - 21 六月, 2018
      </div>
      <div class="afd-post-content " itemprop="articleBody">
       <figure aria-labelledby="figcaption_newsroom-picture-att-id-5b281898f197cce0d7000044" class="js-image-size media-picture" data-height="336" data-width="640" id="newsroom-picture-att-id-5b281898f197cce0d7000044" style="width: 640px; height: 336px;">
        <a class="js-image-size__link lazy-anchor" href="/cn/896688/na-zuo-cheng-shi-yong-you-zui-duo-gao-ceng-jian-zhu" rel="attachment" style="width: 640px; height: 336px;">
         <img alt="哪座城市拥有最多高层建筑？" class="b-lazy" data-nr-picture-id="5b281898f197cce0d7000044" data-src="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5b28/1898/f197/cce0/d700/0044/newsletter/CITYFINAL.jpg?1529354379" data-src-small="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5b28/1898/f197/cce0/d700/0044/medium_jpg/CITYFINAL.jpg?1529354379" itemprop="image" longdesc="https://www.archdaily.cn/cn/896688/na-zuo-cheng-shi-yong-you-zui-duo-gao-ceng-jian-zhu/5b281898f197cce0d7000044-which-cities-have-the-most-high-rises-image" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAUEBAAAACwAAAAAAQABAAACAkQBADs="/>
        </a>
        <figcaption class="figcaption afd-desktop-e" id="figcaption_newsroom-picture-att-id-5b281898f197cce0d7000044">
        </figcaption>
        <i class="figcaption-icon afd-desktop-e">
        </i>
       </figure>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
        一座城市的天际线恐怕是这座城市最具象征意义的特征。 我们所熟悉和喜爱的城市标志性景观通常都是由一座座摩天大楼构成的，但其周围还会建有许多其他的高层建筑。的确，摩天大楼和高层建筑之间是有区别的。专门研究高层建筑的 Emporis 研究公司将高层建筑定义为高度至少35米，或12层以上高的建筑。这些高层建筑在当今大城市复杂的环境中扮演着重要的角色。
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
        看了 Emporis 公司列出的世界上20个高层建筑最多的城市。你可能会惊讶于那些上榜的城市。
       </p>
       <p class="thumbs afd-desktop-e clearfix">
        <a class="thumbs__link" data-nr-picture-id="5b234445f197ccfa27000192" href="/cn/896688/na-zuo-cheng-shi-yong-you-zui-duo-gao-ceng-jian-zhu/5b234445f197ccfa27000192-which-cities-have-the-most-high-rises-image" rel="attachment">
         <img alt="哪座城市拥有最多高层建筑？" class="thumbs__img b-lazy" data-nr-picture-id="5b234445f197ccfa27000192" data-pin-nopin="true" data-src="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5b23/4445/f197/ccfa/2700/0192/thumb_jpg/highrisefeature.jpg?1529037886" height="125" longdesc="https://www.archdaily.cn/cn/896688/na-zuo-cheng-shi-yong-you-zui-duo-gao-ceng-jian-zhu/5b234445f197ccfa27000192-which-cities-have-the-most-high-rises-image" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw==" title="" width="125"/>
        </a>
        <a class="thumbs__link" data-nr-picture-id="5b230d45f197ccfa2700015a" href="/cn/896688/na-zuo-cheng-shi-yong-you-zui-duo-gao-ceng-jian-zhu/5b230d45f197ccfa2700015a-which-cities-have-the-most-high-rises-image" rel="attachment">

        </a>
        <a class="thumbs__link" data-nr-picture-id="5b230dd7f197ccfa27000160" href="/cn/896688/na-zuo-cheng-shi-yong-you-zui-duo-gao-ceng-jian-zhu/5b230dd7f197ccfa27000160-which-cities-have-the-most-high-rises-image" rel="attachment">

        </a>

      <div class="custom-tag-streamlogo">
      </div>
      <h3 class="afd-title-big afd-title-big--bmargin-small afd-mobile-margin">
       <a class="afd-title--black-link" href="/cn/896503/jian-zhu-shi-bi-bei-zhi-shi-ru-he-li-yong-se-cai-xin-li-xue-she-ji-jian-zhu">
        <span itemprop="name">
         建筑师必备知识，如何利用色彩心理学设计建筑？
        </span>
       </a>
      </h3>
      <div class="date-publication afd-mobile-margin">
       <meta content="2018-06-21" itemprop="datePublished"/>
       12:30 - 21 六月, 2018
      </div>
      <div class="afd-post-content " itemprop="articleBody">
       <figure aria-labelledby="figcaption_newsroom-picture-att-id-5af9345ef197cc525a0000c3" class="js-image-size media-picture" data-height="426" data-width="640" id="newsroom-picture-att-id-5af9345ef197cc525a0000c3" style="width: 640px; height: 426px;">
        <a class="js-image-size__link lazy-anchor" href="/cn/896503/jian-zhu-shi-bi-bei-zhi-shi-ru-he-li-yong-se-cai-xin-li-xue-she-ji-jian-zhu" rel="attachment" style="width: 640px; height: 426px;">
         <img alt="建筑师必备知识，如何利用色彩心理学设计建筑？, Escola em Alto de Pinheiros / Base Urbana + Pessoa Arquitetos. Image © Pedro Vanucchi" class="b-lazy" data-nr-picture-id="5af9345ef197cc525a0000c3" data-src="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5af9/345e/f197/cc52/5a00/00c3/newsletter/Escola_em_Alto_de_Pinheiros_Pedro_Vanucchi.jpg?1526281304" data-src-small="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5af9/345e/f197/cc52/5a00/00c3/medium_jpg/Escola_em_Alto_de_Pinheiros_Pedro_Vanucchi.jpg?1526281304" itemprop="image" longdesc="https://www.archdaily.cn/cn/896503/jian-zhu-shi-bi-bei-zhi-shi-ru-he-li-yong-se-cai-xin-li-xue-she-ji-jian-zhu/5af9345ef197cc525a0000c3-the-role-of-color-in-architecture-visual-effects-and-psychological-stimuli-photo" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAUEBAAAACwAAAAAAQABAAACAkQBADs="/>
        </a>
        <figcaption class="figcaption afd-desktop-e" id="figcaption_newsroom-picture-att-id-5af9345ef197cc525a0000c3">
         Escola em Alto de Pinheiros / Base Urbana + Pessoa Arquitetos. Image © Pedro Vanucchi
        </figcaption>
        <i class="figcaption-cc-icon afd-desktop-e">
        </i>
       </figure>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
        颜色和我们对颜色的认知是一系列精神空间关系的意识和潜意识刺激的根源。尽管它时有时无，不断变换，它仍然存在于任何地方。你有没有想过它在建筑中的作用是什么?
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
        除了构成建筑物体的结构元素之外，色彩在建筑表面的应用也会影响使用者对空间的体验。根据 Israel Pedrosa 的说法，“色觉是由一种物质折射或反射光的细微差别所产生的，颜色这个词通常被指定为在色觉中起刺激作用的那些色调。”[1]
       </p>
      </div>
      <div class="hidden">
       <span itemprop="url">
        https://www.archdaily.cn/cn/896503/jian-zhu-shi-bi-bei-zhi-shi-ru-he-li-yong-se-cai-xin-li-xue-she-ji-jian-zhu
       </span>
       <span itemprop="author" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        Matheus Pereira
       </span>
      </div>
      <ul class="stream-socialbar clearfix afd-mobile-margin">
       <li class="streamPost-bookmark">

         <i class="afd-icon-text__icon afd-icon afd-icon--icon-folder-blue">
         </i>
         <span class="afd-fl">
          收藏文章
         </span>
        </a>

      <h3 class="afd-title-big afd-title-big--bmargin-small afd-mobile-margin">
       <a class="afd-title--black-link" href="/cn/896744/mo-gan-shan-anadu-du-jia-jiu-dian-ba-huang-she-ji">
        <span itemprop="name">
         莫干山 Anadu 度假酒店 / 八荒设计
        </span>
       </a>
      </h3>
      <div class="date-publication afd-mobile-margin">
       <meta content="2018-06-21" itemprop="datePublished"/>
       10:30 - 21 六月, 2018
      </div>
      <div class="afd-post-content " itemprop="articleBody">
       <figure aria-labelledby="figcaption_newsroom-picture-att-id-5b29afe9f197cc4f8a000144" class="js-image-size media-picture" data-height="426" data-width="640" id="newsroom-picture-att-id-5b29afe9f197cc4f8a000144" style="width: 640px; height: 426px;">
        <a class="js-image-size__link lazy-anchor" href="/cn/896744/mo-gan-shan-anadu-du-jia-jiu-dian-ba-huang-she-ji" rel="attachment" style="width: 640px; height: 426px;">
         <img alt="莫干山 Anadu 度假酒店 / 八荒设计, 建筑。图片致谢 © 张大齐" class="b-lazy" data-nr-picture-id="5b29afe9f197cc4f8a000144" data-src="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5b29/afe9/f197/cc4f/8a00/0144/newsletter/architecture_02.jpg?1529458651" data-src-small="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5b29/afe9/f197/cc4f/8a00/0144/medium_jpg/architecture_02.jpg?1529458651" itemprop="image" longdesc="https://www.archdaily.cn/cn/896744/mo-gan-shan-anadu-du-jia-jiu-dian-ba-huang-she-ji/5b29afe9f197cc4f8a000144-mo-gan-shan-anadu-du-jia-jiu-dian-ba-huang-she-ji-zhao-pian" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAUEBAAAACwAAAAAAQABAAACAkQBADs="/>
        </a>
        <figcaption class="figcaption afd-desktop-e" id="figcaption_newsroom-picture-att-id-5b29afe9f197cc4f8a000144">
         建筑。图片致谢 © 张大齐
        </figcaption>
        <i class="figcaption-cc-icon afd-desktop-e">
        </i>
       </figure>

     <div class="afd-post-stream clearfix " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">
      <div class="custom-tag-streamlogo">
      </div>
      <h3 class="afd-title-big afd-title-big--bmargin-small afd-mobile-margin">
       <a class="afd-title--black-link" href="/cn/896746/yue-han-star-bo-te-man-shi-wu-suo-zui-xin-xiao-xi-sheng-chu-wu-xi-chao-gao-ceng-ta-lou-jing-sai">
        <span itemprop="name">
         约翰·波特曼事务所最新消息，胜出无锡超高层塔楼竞赛
        </span>
       </a>
      </h3>
      <div class="date-publication afd-mobile-margin">
       <meta content="2018-06-21" itemprop="datePublished"/>
       09:00 - 21 六月, 2018
      </div>
      <div class="afd-post-content " itemprop="articleBody">
       <figure aria-labelledby="5b202ae5f197cc0f930001ae" class="js-image-size media-picture" data-height="510" data-width="640" style="width: 640px; height: 510px;">
        <a class="js-image-size__link lazy-anchor" href="/cn/896746/yue-han-star-bo-te-man-shi-wu-suo-zui-xin-xiao-xi-sheng-chu-wu-xi-chao-gao-ceng-ta-lou-jing-sai" style="width: 640px; height: 510px;">
         <img alt="Courtesy of John Portman &amp; Associates" class="b-lazy" data-src="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5b20/2ae5/f197/cc0f/9300/01ae/newsletter/43695-main_3258-3_43695_sc_v2com.jpg?1528834775" data-src-small="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5b20/2ae5/f197/cc0f/9300/01ae/medium_jpg/43695-main_3258-3_43695_sc_v2com.jpg?1528834775" itemprop="image" longdesc="https://www.archdaily.cn/cn/896746/yue-han-star-bo-te-man-shi-wu-suo-zui-xin-xiao-xi-sheng-chu-wu-xi-chao-gao-ceng-ta-lou-jing-sai/5b202ae5f197cc0f930001ae-john-portman-and-associates-wins-design-competition-for-super-tall-tower-in-wuxi-china-image" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAUEBAAAACwAAAAAAQABAAACAkQBADs="/>
        </a>
        <figcaption class="figcaption afd-desktop-e" id="5b202ae5f197cc0f930001ae">
         Courtesy of John Portman &amp; Associates
        </figcaption>
        <i class="figcaption-icon afd-desktop-e">
        </i>
       </figure>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
        约翰波特曼建筑设计事务所，继去年年底创始人约翰·波特曼的离世后，依旧延续事务所在酒店设计的优势，在日前公布了在中国无锡西水东A地块超高层项目的设计“绿地无锡200”，并赢得了由绿地（香港）组织的国际设计竞赛。该塔楼设定高度为200米，楼内将包括铂瑞酒店、loft形式的公寓以及空中云墅。
       </p>
      </div>
      <div class="hidden">
       <span itemprop="url">
        https://www.archdaily.cn/cn/896746/yue-han-star-bo-te-man-shi-wu-suo-zui-xin-xiao-xi-sheng-chu-wu-xi-chao-gao-ceng-ta-lou-jing-sai
       </span>
       <span itemprop="author" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        Ella Comberg
       </span>
      </div>

      <h3 class="afd-title-big afd-title-big--bmargin-small afd-mobile-margin">
       <a class="afd-title--black-link" href="/cn/896836/open-she-ji-shen-zhen-ping-shan-yan-yi-zhong-xin-jun-gong-zai-ji-xi-ju-fang-he-tu-po-chuan-tong-ju-yuan-xing-shi">
        <span itemprop="name">
         OPEN 设计‘深圳坪山演艺中心’竣工在即，戏剧方盒突破传统剧院形式
        </span>
       </a>
      </h3>
      <div class="date-publication afd-mobile-margin">
       <meta content="2018-06-21" itemprop="datePublished"/>
       08:00 - 21 六月, 2018
      </div>
      <div class="afd-post-content " itemprop="articleBody">
       <figure aria-labelledby="figcaption_newsroom-picture-att-id-5b2b5281f197ccb76c0002f5" class="js-image-size media-picture" data-height="426" data-width="640" id="newsroom-picture-att-id-5b2b5281f197ccb76c0002f5" style="width: 640px; height: 426px;">
        <a class="js-image-size__link lazy-anchor" href="/cn/896836/open-she-ji-shen-zhen-ping-shan-yan-yi-zhong-xin-jun-gong-zai-ji-xi-ju-fang-he-tu-po-chuan-tong-ju-yuan-xing-shi" rel="attachment" style="width: 640px; height: 426px;">
         <img alt="OPEN 设计‘深圳坪山演艺中心’竣工在即，戏剧方盒突破传统剧院形式, © 张超" class="b-lazy" data-nr-picture-id="5b2b5281f197ccb76c0002f5" data-src="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5b2b/5281/f197/ccb7/6c00/02f5/newsletter/OPEN_Pingshan_02.jpg?1529565818" data-src-small="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5b2b/5281/f197/ccb7/6c00/02f5/medium_jpg/OPEN_Pingshan_02.jpg?1529565818" itemprop="image" longdesc="https://www.archdaily.cn/cn/896836/open-she-ji-shen-zhen-ping-shan-yan-yi-zhong-xin-jun-gong-zai-ji-xi-ju-fang-he-tu-po-chuan-tong-ju-yuan-xing-shi/5b2b5281f197ccb76c0002f5-open-she-ji-shen-zhen-ping-shan-yan-yi-zhong-xin-jun-gong-zai-ji-xi-ju-fang-he-tu-po-chuan-tong-ju-yuan-xing-shi-zhao-pian" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAUEBAAAACwAAAAAAQABAAACAkQBADs="/>
        </a>
        <figcaption class="figcaption afd-desktop-e" id="figcaption_newsroom-picture-att-id-5b2b5281f197ccb76c0002f5">
         © 张超
        </figcaption>
        <i class="figcaption-cc-icon afd-desktop-e">
        </i>
       </figure>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
        近日，由
        <a href="https://www.archdaily.cn/cn/office/openjian-zhu-shi-wu-suo">
         OPEN 建筑事务所
        </a>
        设计的
        <a href="https://www.archdaily.com/599263/construction-begins-on-open-s-pingshan-performing-arts-center-in-shenzhen" target="_blank">
         深圳坪山演艺中心
        </a>
        即将竣工。目前已完成立面幕墙的安装，接下来将进行室内和景观施工阶段。
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
        坪山演艺中心是在中国语境下的一个非典型剧院案例。设计旨在脱离单一功能的文化地标型建筑，策略性地引入并重新组织文化观演、公众活动等功能。建筑的中心功能是一个1200座的剧场，周围围绕公共步道系统，并且将一系列多尺度的室内外空间串联起来，包括排练房、舞蹈教室、黑盒子小剧场、咖啡厅、餐厅和室外花园等。
       </p>
       <p class="thumbs afd-desktop-e clearfix">
        <a class="thumbs__link" data-nr-picture-id="5b2b529ef197ccb76c0002fd" href="/cn/896836/open-she-ji-shen-zhen-ping-shan-yan-yi-zhong-xin-jun-gong-zai-ji-xi-ju-fang-he-tu-po-chuan-tong-ju-yuan-xing-shi/5b2b529ef197ccb76c0002fd-open-she-ji-shen-zhen-ping-shan-yan-yi-zhong-xin-jun-gong-zai-ji-xi-ju-fang-he-tu-po-chuan-tong-ju-yuan-xing-shi-zhao-pian" rel="attachment">
         <img alt="© 张超" class="thumbs__img b-lazy" data-nr-picture-id="5b2b529ef197ccb76c0002fd" data-pin-nopin="true" data-src="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5b2b/529e/f197/ccb7/6c00/02fd/thumb_jpg/OPEN_Pingshan_06.jpg?1529565848" height="125" longdesc="https://www.archdaily.cn/cn/896836/open-she-ji-shen-zhen-ping-shan-yan-yi-zhong-xin-jun-gong-zai-ji-xi-ju-fang-he-tu-po-chuan-tong-ju-yuan-xing-shi/5b2b529ef197ccb76c0002fd-open-she-ji-shen-zhen-ping-shan-yan-yi-zhong-xin-jun-gong-zai-ji-xi-ju-fang-he-tu-po-chuan-tong-ju-yuan-xing-shi-zhao-pian" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw==" title="© 张超" width="125"/>
        </a>

        </a>

      <div class="custom-tag-streamlogo">
      </div>
      <h3 class="afd-title-big afd-title-big--bmargin-small afd-mobile-margin">
       <a class="afd-title--black-link" href="/cn/896117/gei-jian-zhu-shi-zui-bang-de-app">
        <span itemprop="name">
         给建筑师最棒的APP
        </span>
       </a>
      </h3>
      <div class="date-publication afd-mobile-margin">
       <meta content="2018-06-20" itemprop="datePublished"/>
       15:30 - 20 六月, 2018
      </div>
      <div class="afd-post-content " itemprop="articleBody">
       <figure aria-labelledby="figcaption_newsroom-picture-att-id-5b1e014bf197cce713000042" class="js-image-size media-picture" data-height="426" data-width="640" id="newsroom-picture-att-id-5b1e014bf197cce713000042" style="width: 640px; height: 426px;">
        <a class="js-image-size__link lazy-anchor" href="/cn/896117/gei-jian-zhu-shi-zui-bang-de-app" rel="attachment" style="width: 640px; height: 426px;">
         <img alt="给建筑师最棒的APP, Morpholio Trace. Work displayed by Sean Gallagher of Diller Scofidio + Renfro." class="b-lazy" data-nr-picture-id="5b1e014bf197cce713000042" data-src="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5b1e/014b/f197/cce7/1300/0042/newsletter/170619_ArchDaily_DSR_Sean_06_Construction_Docs.jpg?1528693061" data-src-small="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5b1e/014b/f197/cce7/1300/0042/medium_jpg/170619_ArchDaily_DSR_Sean_06_Construction_Docs.jpg?1528693061" itemprop="image" longdesc="https://www.archdaily.cn/cn/896117/gei-jian-zhu-shi-zui-bang-de-app/5b1e014bf197cce713000042-gei-jian-zhu-shi-zui-bang-de-app-tu-xiang" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAUEBAAAACwAAAAAAQABAAACAkQBADs="/>
        </a>
        <figcaption class="figcaption afd-desktop-e" id="figcaption_newsroom-picture-att-id-5b1e014bf197cce713000042">
         Morpholio Trace. Work displayed by Sean Gallagher of Diller Scofidio + Renfro.
        </figcaption>
        <i class="figcaption-icon afd-desktop-e">
        </i>
       </figure>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
        我们都知道在建筑界中更有经验的从业者在谈到技术时常说的一句话：“时间会对我们来说会更难，”他们会告诉你的。 “我们过去常常手工绘制所有东西，犯了一个错误就意味着从头开始重复一切，你这一代人被宠坏了。”
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
        “被宠坏”也许只是一个观点。 但是，现在在建筑领域工作与几十年前相比是完全不同的。 软件开发人员（或者我们喜欢称之为“救命的人”）已经写出来了允许我们加强我们的建筑的软件和 app。 但有了这么多的 app，可能很难跟上步伐。 为了帮助你，下面列出了目前在应用市场上的最好的建筑 app。
       </p>
      </div>
      <div class="hidden">
       <span itemprop="url">
        https://www.archdaily.cn/cn/896117/gei-jian-zhu-shi-zui-bang-de-app
       </span>
       <span itemprop="author" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        Dima Stouhi
       </span>
      </div>
      <ul class="stream-socialbar clearfix afd-mobile-margin">
       <li class="streamPost-bookmark">

         <i class="afd-icon-text__icon afd-icon afd-icon--icon-folder-blue">
         </i>
         <span class="afd-fl">
          收藏文章
         </span>
        </a>
       </li>
       <li class="stream-socialbar__more">

        <a href="/cn/896543/ge-ben-ha-gen-she-xing-zi-xing-che-dao-dissing-plus-weitling-architecture" title="哥本哈根蛇形自行车道/ DISSING+WEITLING Architecture">
         阅读更多 »
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
     </div>
     <div class="afd-post-stream clearfix " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">
      <div class="custom-tag-streamlogo">
      </div>
      <h3 class="afd-title-big afd-title-big--bmargin-small afd-mobile-margin">
       <a class="afd-title--black-link" href="/cn/896605/quan-qiu-15ge-jian-zhu-xue-yuan-da-lou-he-ji-pei-yu-jian-zhu-shi-de-kong-jian-du-you-na-xie-chuang-yi-an-li">
        <span itemprop="name">
         全球15个建筑学院大楼合集，培育建筑师的空间都有哪些创意案例？
        </span>
       </a>
      </h3>
      <div class="date-publication afd-mobile-margin">
       <meta content="2018-06-20" itemprop="datePublished"/>
       13:30 - 20 六月, 2018
      </div>
      <div class="afd-post-content " itemprop="articleBody">
       <figure aria-labelledby="5b22d3d7f197ccfa270000f3" class="js-image-size media-picture" data-height="425" data-width="640" style="width: 640px; height: 425px;">
        <a class="js-image-size__link lazy-anchor" href="/cn/896605/quan-qiu-15ge-jian-zhu-xue-yuan-da-lou-he-ji-pei-yu-jian-zhu-shi-de-kong-jian-du-you-na-xie-chuang-yi-an-li" style="width: 640px; height: 425px;">
         <img alt="© Matthew Carbone" class="b-lazy" data-src="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5b22/d3d7/f197/ccfa/2700/00f3/newsletter/Milstein.jpg?1529009106" data-src-small="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5b22/d3d7/f197/ccfa/2700/00f3/medium_jpg/Milstein.jpg?1529009106" itemprop="image" longdesc="https://www.archdaily.cn/cn/896605/quan-qiu-15ge-jian-zhu-xue-yuan-da-lou-he-ji-pei-yu-jian-zhu-shi-de-kong-jian-du-you-na-xie-chuang-yi-an-li/5b22d3d7f197ccfa270000f3-15-inspiring-architecture-school-buildings-from-around-the-world-photo" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAUEBAAAACwAAAAAAQABAAACAkQBADs="/>
        </a>
        <figcaption class="figcaption afd-desktop-e" id="5b22d3d7f197ccfa270000f3">
         © Matthew Carbone
        </figcaption>
        <i class="figcaption-cc-icon afd-desktop-e">
        </i>
       </figure>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p dir="ltr">
        建筑系学生所处的建筑学院大楼与他们有着一段独特而有趣的“建筑－用户”的关系。在建筑系学生眼里，他们的系大楼不仅是实现设计工作室项目的一个必要场所，而且一个实用建筑的案例和模型。由于建筑是建筑系学生首要接触，阅读，和理解何为建筑的地方，因此校园建筑设计成为全套教学工具帮助新设计师掌握结构，细节，材料如何表现和互动，以及建筑的其他核心概念。虽然学生和教师的评审制度已经十分全面了，但建筑师还是接受了许多既符合学校具体需求又引人入胜的教学，并通过实例让学生接受更多教学实战。
       </p>
      </div>
      <div class="hidden">
       <span itemprop="url">
        https://www.archdaily.cn/cn/896605/quan-qiu-15ge-jian-zhu-xue-yuan-da-lou-he-ji-pei-yu-jian-zhu-shi-de-kong-jian-du-you-na-xie-chuang-yi-an-li
       </span>
       <span itemprop="author" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        Jack McManus
       </span>
      </div>
      <ul class="stream-socialbar clearfix afd-mobile-margin">
       <li class="streamPost-bookmark">
        <a class="afd-icon-text afd-save-item clearfix js-myad-multiple-fav" data-image="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5b22/ced2/f197/ccfa/2700/00db/medium_jpg/ARCHSCHOOL.jpg?1529007813" data-message="收藏文章" data-title="全球15个建筑学院大楼合集，培育建筑师的空间都有哪些创意案例？" href="https://www.archdaily.cn/cn/896605/quan-qiu-15ge-jian-zhu-xue-yuan-da-lou-he-ji-pei-yu-jian-zhu-shi-de-kong-jian-du-you-na-xie-chuang-yi-an-li">
         <i class="afd-icon-text__icon afd-icon afd-icon--icon-folder-blue">
         </i>
         <span class="afd-fl">
          收藏文章
         </span>
        </a>
       </li>
       <li class="stream-socialbar__more">

     <div class="afd-post-stream clearfix " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">
      <div class="custom-tag-streamlogo">
      </div>
      <h3 class="afd-title-big afd-title-big--bmargin-small afd-mobile-margin">
       <a class="afd-title--black-link" href="/cn/896071/niu-yue-shi-chang-jue-xin-zai-2026nian-qian-ti-gong-30mo-hu-jing-ji-yong-fang-wo-men-ke-yi-xue-dao-shi-yao">
        <span itemprop="name">
         纽约市长拟在2026年前提供30万户经济用房，计划书有哪些看点?
        </span>
       </a>
      </h3>
      <div class="date-publication afd-mobile-margin">
       <meta content="2018-06-20" itemprop="datePublished"/>
       12:30 - 20 六月, 2018
      </div>
      <div class="afd-post-content " itemprop="articleBody">
       <figure aria-labelledby="figcaption_newsroom-picture-att-id-5b112bd7f197ccd782000234" class="js-image-size media-picture" data-height="426" data-width="640" id="newsroom-picture-att-id-5b112bd7f197ccd782000234" style="width: 640px; height: 426px;">
        <a class="js-image-size__link lazy-anchor" href="/cn/896071/niu-yue-shi-chang-jue-xin-zai-2026nian-qian-ti-gong-30mo-hu-jing-ji-yong-fang-wo-men-ke-yi-xue-dao-shi-yao" rel="attachment" style="width: 640px; height: 426px;">
         <img alt="纽约市长拟在2026年前提供30万户经济用房，计划书有哪些看点?, Broadway Housing in Santa Monica, by Kevin Daly, was identified by the report as a case study for its circulation. Image © Iwan Baan" class="b-lazy" data-nr-picture-id="5b112bd7f197ccd782000234" data-src="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5b11/2bd7/f197/ccd7/8200/0234/newsletter/PORTADA.jpg?1527851983" data-src-small="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5b11/2bd7/f197/ccd7/8200/0234/medium_jpg/PORTADA.jpg?1527851983" itemprop="image" longdesc="https://www.archdaily.cn/cn/896071/niu-yue-shi-chang-jue-xin-zai-2026nian-qian-ti-gong-30mo-hu-jing-ji-yong-fang-wo-men-ke-yi-xue-dao-shi-yao/5b112bd7f197ccd782000234-7-lessons-from-new-yorks-new-affordable-housing-design-guide-photo" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAUEBAAAACwAAAAAAQABAAACAkQBADs="/>
        </a>
        <figcaption class="figcaption afd-desktop-e" id="figcaption_newsroom-picture-att-id-5b112bd7f197ccd782000234">
         Broadway Housing in Santa Monica, by Kevin Daly, was identified by the report as a case study for its circulation. Image © Iwan Baan
        </figcaption>
        <i class="figcaption-cc-icon afd-desktop-e">
        </i>
       </figure>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
        当我们想到美国的
        <a href="https://www.archdaily.com/tag/public-housing" target="_blank">
         公共住房
        </a>
        建筑时，往往会想到盒子：没有太多美学特征的大型砖石建筑。不过对居住者而言，标准化的配有荧光照明的高楼带来的影响远远超越了一般的美学价值。举个例子，地理学者 Rashad Shabazz 在他名为 “
        <a href="https://www.press.uillinois.edu/books/catalog/52nwq3by9780252039645.html" target="_blank">
         Spatializing Blackness
        </a>
        ” 的书中回忆说，他在芝加哥的一栋住房里长大，房子被链式栅栏围住，视频监控和金属探测器无处不在，那种感觉更像是监狱而不是家。来自全国各地的居住在公共住房中的居民纷纷反映了居住环境隔离，限制重重和维护不善等情况。
       </p>
       <p>
       </p>
       <p>
        但美国的
        <a href="https://www.archdaily.com/tag/public-housing" target="_blank">
         公共住房
        </a>
        不一定非得如此荒凉。
        <a href="https://www.archdaily.com/tag/nyc-public-design-commission" target="_blank">
         纽约市公共设计委员会 (New York City Public Design Commission/PDC)
        </a>
        与
        <a href="http://fineartsfederation.org/" target="_blank">
         纽约美术联合会 (The Fine Arts Federation of New York)
        </a>
        以及
        <a href="https://www.aiany.org/" target="_blank">
         美国建筑师学会纽约分会 (American Institute of Architects New York Chapter)
        </a>
        联合制定了一套新设计标准，希望能够翻开经济适用住房建筑的新篇章。
       </p>
       <p class="thumbs afd-desktop-e clearfix">
        <a class="thumbs__link" data-nr-picture-id="5b112ef9f197ccd78200023b" href="/cn/896071/niu-yue-shi-chang-jue-xin-zai-2026nian-qian-ti-gong-30mo-hu-jing-ji-yong-fang-wo-men-ke-yi-xue-dao-shi-yao/5b112ef9f197ccd78200023b-7-lessons-from-new-yorks-new-affordable-housing-design-guide-image" rel="attachment">
         <img alt="Step Up on Fifth in Santa Monica, by Brooks + Scarpa, was identified by the report as a case study for its windows and doors. Image Courtesy of Brooks + Scarpa" class="thumbs__img b-lazy" data-nr-picture-id="5b112ef9f197ccd78200023b" data-pin-nopin="true" data-src="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5b11/2ef9/f197/ccd7/8200/023b/thumb_jpg/stringio.jpg?1527852788" height="125" longdesc="https://www.archdaily.cn/cn/896071/niu-yue-shi-chang-jue-xin-zai-2026nian-qian-ti-gong-30mo-hu-jing-ji-yong-fang-wo-men-ke-yi-xue-dao-shi-yao/5b112ef9f197ccd78200023b-7-lessons-from-new-yorks-new-affordable-housing-design-guide-image" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw==" title="Step Up on Fifth in Santa Monica, by Brooks + Scarpa, was identified by the report as a case study for its windows and doors. Image Courtesy of Brooks + Scarpa" width="125"/>
        </a>
        <a class="thumbs__link" data-nr-picture-id="5b112eb3f197ccd782000236" href="/cn/896071/niu-yue-shi-chang-jue-xin-zai-2026nian-qian-ti-gong-30mo-hu-jing-ji-yong-fang-wo-men-ke-yi-xue-dao-shi-yao/5b112eb3f197ccd782000236-7-lessons-from-new-yorks-new-affordable-housing-design-guide-photo" rel="attachment">
         <img alt="The Navy Green development in Brooklyn was a key case study in the report. Here, the supportive housing from that development, designed by Architecture in Formation and Curtis + Ginsburg. Image © Tom Powel Imaging" class="thumbs__img b-lazy" data-nr-picture-id="5b112eb3f197ccd782000236" data-pin-nopin="true" data-src="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5b11/2eb3/f197/ccd7/8200/0236/thumb_jpg/Navy_Green_entry_HR_(w2880px).jpg?1527852711" height="125" longdesc="https://www.archdaily.cn/cn/896071/niu-yue-shi-chang-jue-xin-zai-2026nian-qian-ti-gong-30mo-hu-jing-ji-yong-fang-wo-men-ke-yi-xue-dao-shi-yao/5b112eb3f197ccd782000236-7-lessons-from-new-yorks-new-affordable-housing-design-guide-photo" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw==" title="The Navy Green development in Brooklyn was a key case study in the report. Here, the supportive housing from that development, designed by Architecture in Formation and Curtis + Ginsburg. Image © Tom Powel Imaging" width="125"/>
        </a>
        <a class="thumbs__link" data-nr-picture-id="5b112ea2f197ccd782000235" href="/cn/896071/niu-yue-shi-chang-jue-xin-zai-2026nian-qian-ti-gong-30mo-hu-jing-ji-yong-fang-wo-men-ke-yi-xue-dao-shi-yao/5b112ea2f197ccd782000235-7-lessons-from-new-yorks-new-affordable-housing-design-guide-image" rel="attachment">
         <img alt="The Tetris Apartments in Ljubljana, by OFIS Arhitekti, were identified by the report as a case study for their massing. Image Courtesy of OFIS Arhitekti" class="thumbs__img b-lazy" data-nr-picture-id="5b112ea2f197ccd782000235" data-pin-nopin="true" data-src="http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5b11/2ea2/f197/ccd7/8200/0235/thumb_jpg/stringio_(2).jpg?1527852699" height="125" longdesc="https://www.archdaily.cn/cn/896071/niu-yue-shi-chang-jue-xin-zai-2026nian-qian-ti-gong-30mo-hu-jing-ji-yong-fang-wo-men-ke-yi-xue-dao-shi-yao/5b112ea2f197ccd782000235-7-lessons-from-new-yorks-new-affordable-housing-design-guide-image" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAAAAACH5BAEKAAEALAAAAAABAAEAAAICTAEAOw==" title="The Tetris Apartments in Ljubljana, by OFIS Arhitekti, were identified by the report as a case study for their massing. Image Courtesy of OFIS Arhitekti" width="125"/>
        </a>
        <a class="thumbs__link" data-nr-picture-id="5b15e643f197ccb528000046" href="/cn/896071/niu-yue-shi-chang-jue-xin-zai-2026nian-qian-ti-gong-30mo-hu-jing-ji-yong-fang-wo-men-ke-yi-xue-dao-shi-yao/5b15e643f197ccb528000046-7-lessons-from-new-yorks-new-affordable-housing-design-guide-image" rel="attachment">
         <img alt="Creston Avenue Residence in the Bronx.         </a>
        <a class="gallery-link afd-desktop-e" href="/cn/896071/niu-yue-shi-chang-jue-xin-zai-2026nian-qian-ti-gong-30mo-hu-jing-ji-yong-fang-wo-men-ke-yi-xue-dao-shi-yao/5b112bd7f197ccd782000234-7-lessons-from-new-yorks-new-affordable-housing-design-guide-photo" style='background-image: url("http://images.adsttc.com.qtlcn.com/media/images/5b11/2bd7/f197/ccd7/8200/0234/newsletter/PORTADA.jpg?1527851983")'>

/* Polyfill for IE based browsers */
if (!String.prototype.includes) {
  String.prototype.includes = function(search, start) {
    if (typeof start !== 'number') {
      start = 0;
    }

    if (start + search.length > this.length) {
      return false;
    } else {
      return this.indexOf(search, start) !== -1;
    }
  };
}

/* utils function */
var parse_errors = function(data) {
  if (data != undefined)
    data = JSON.parse(data);
  if (data['errors']) {
    return data['errors'].reduce(function(acc, val) {
      if (val === Object(val)) {
        for (var key in val) {
          if (val.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
            return acc + '- ' + key + ': ' + val[key] + "\n";
          }
        }
      } else
        return acc + '- ' + val + "\n";
    }, '');
  }
  return '';
}
function validateEmail(email) {
  var re = /^(([^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+(\.[^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+)*)|(\".+\"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
  return re.test(email);
}

/*! adauth v0.9 */
var AD = {
  CurrentUser: {
    id: null,
    email: null,
    full_name: null,
    accepted_at: null
  },
  invited: false,
  modalOpened: false,
  initialized: false //this means that the user has not called AD.init yet
};

// Allows to initialize the Kenneth JS SDK. Use this method to change default parameters with your
// in the library.
AD.init = function(options) {
  this.reload_on_login = options.reload_on_login === undefined ? true : options.reload_on_login;
  this.reload_on_logout = options.reload_on_logout === undefined ? true : options.reload_on_logout;
  this.auto_open = options.auto_open === undefined ? false : options.auto_open;
  this.redirect_uri = options.redirect_uri || null;
  this.site = options.site || 'us';
  this.domain = options.domain;
  this.callback = options.callback || null
  this.cookie_ttl = 240000;
  this.use_cookie = options.use_cookie === undefined ? true : options.use_cookie;
  this.initialized = true;
  this.logout_options = options.logout_options || null;
  this.show_confirmation_alert = options.show_confirmation_alert === undefined ? true : options.show_confirmation_alert;
  this.enable_signup = options.enable_signup === undefined ? true : options.enable_signup;
  // internal uris
  this.prepend_api = options.prepend_api || '';
  this.sign_in_uri = this.prepend_api+ '/accounts/sign_in';
  this.sign_up_uri = this.prepend_api + '/accounts/sign_up';
  this.sign_out_uri = this.prepend_api + '/accounts/sign_out' + '?site=' + this.site;
  this.profile_uri = this.prepend_api + '/accounts/profile' + '?site=' + this.site;
  this.resend_confirmation_email_uri = this.prepend_api + '/accounts/resend_confirmation_mail' + '?site=' + this.site;
  this.check_uri = this.prepend_api + '/accounts/check' + '?site=' + this.site;
  this.delete_uri = this.prepend_api + '/users/unsubscribe?site=' + this.site;
  this.accept_terms_uri = '/auth/accounts/accept_terms?site=' + this.site;
  this.goodbye_uri = this.prepend_api + '/users/goodbye?site=' + this.site;
  this.template_welcome_uri = '/auth/assets/welcome';
  this.template_me_uri = '/auth/assets/me';
  this.template_forgot_uri = '/auth/assets/forgot';
  this.template_invite = '/auth/assets/invite';
  this.profile_type = options.profile_type || 'minimal'; // it can be minimal or full.
}

// Checks legacy token to compatibilice old Kenneth
AD.legacyCompatibility = function() {
  return $.cookie('adat') !== undefined;
};

// Function to clean the localStorage (of kenneth_me_html) in case we don't have a token to make
// successful requests.
AD.cleanStorage = function() {
  if (AD.localStorageAvailable()) {
    if ($.cookie('ad_session') === undefined && window.localStorage['kth_access_token'] === undefined) {
      window.localStorage.removeItem('kenneth_me_html');
      window.localStorage.removeItem('kenneth_me_html_created_at');
      window.localStorage.removeItem('kth_current_user');
      window.localStorage.removeItem('kenneth_updated_at');
    }
  }
}

AD.device = function() {
  widthWindow = window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth || document.body.clientWidth;
  return widthWindow >= 1040 ? 'desktop' : ( widthWindow >= 768 ? 'tablet' : 'phone');
};

AD.userLang = function() {
  var lang = navigator.language || navigator.userLanguage;
  return lang.toLowerCase();
};

AD.localStorageAvailable = function() {
  var test = 'test';
  try {
      localStorage.setItem(test, test);
      localStorage.removeItem(test);
      return true;
  } catch(e) {
      return false;
  }
};


// returns the current access_token (or null) of the actual user.
AD.getAccessToken = function() {
  if (AD.use_cookie) {
    if ($.cookie('ad_session') != undefined) {
      return $.cookie('ad_session');
    }
    return null;
  } else {
    // We look for the token in the localStorage
    if (AD.localStorageAvailable() && window.localStorage['kth_access_token']) {
      return window.localStorage['kth_access_token'];
    }
    return null;
  }
};

function validateEmailValue(email, validMail, hintMail, validatingForm) {
  var hint = true;

  email.addEventListener('input', function(e) {
    if (validateEmail(email.value)) {
      validMail.classList.add('kth-input-val--true');
      validMail.classList.remove('kth-input-val--false');
      hint = false;
      hintMail.classList.add('afd-hide');
    } else if (email.value == '') {
      validMail.classList.remove('kth-input-val--false');
      validMail.classList.remove('kth-input-val--true');
      hint = true;
    } else {
      validMail.classList.add('kth-input-val--false');
      validMail.classList.remove('kth-input-val--true');
      hint = true;
    }
  });
  email.addEventListener('blur', function(e) {
    if (hint == true) {
      hintMail.classList.remove('afd-hide');
    }
    if (email.value != "" && validatingForm == 'signup')
      AD.check_user_email(email.value, hintMail, validMail);
  });
}

function validatePassLength(pass, validPass, hintPass, forgot) {
  var hint = true;

  pass.addEventListener('input', function(e) {
    if (!!validPass) {
      if (pass.value.length >= 8) {
        validPass.classList.add('kth-input-val--true');
        validPass.classList.remove('kth-input-val--false');
        hint = false;
        hintPass.classList.add('afd-hide');
      } else if (pass.value == '') {
        validPass.classList.remove('kth-input-val--false');
        validPass.classList.remove('kth-input-val--true');
        hint = true;
      } else {
        validPass.classList.add('kth-input-val--false');
        validPass.classList.remove('kth-input-val--true');
        hint = true;
      }
    }
    if (!!forgot) {
      if (pass.value.length >= 3) {
        forgot.classList.remove('kth-forgot--true');
        hint = false;
        hintPass.classList.add('afd-hide');
      } else if (pass.value == '') {
        forgot.classList.remove('kth-forgot--true');
        hint = false;
        hintPass.classList.add('afd-hide');
      } else {
        forgot.classList.add('kth-forgot--true');
        hint = true;
      }
    }
  });
  pass.addEventListener('blur', function(e) {
    if (hint == true) {
      hintPass.classList.remove('afd-hide');
    }
  });
}

function validateName(name, validName, hintName) {
  var hint = true;

  name.addEventListener('input', function(e) {
    if (!!validName) {
      if (name.value.length >= 1) {
        validName.classList.add('kth-input-val--true');
        validName.classList.remove('kth-input-val--false');
        hint = false;
        hintName.classList.add('afd-hide');
      } else if (name.value == '') {
        validName.classList.remove('kth-input-val--false');
        validName.classList.remove('kth-input-val--true');
        hint = true;
      } else {
        validName.classList.add('kth-input-val--false');
        validName.classList.remove('kth-input-val--true');
        hint = true;
      }
    }
  });
  name.addEventListener('blur', function(e) {
    if (hint == true) {
      hintName.classList.remove('afd-hide');
    }
  });
}

function loadingOnSubmit(btn, text) {
  function changeButtonContent() {
    btn.classList.add('kth-loading');
    btn.innerHTML = text;
  }
  btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    changeButtonContent();
  });
  btn.addEventListener("keyup", function(e) {
    if (event.keyCode == 13) {
      changeButtonContent();
    }
  });
}
function removeLoadingOnSubmit(btn, text) {
  btn.classList.remove('kth-loading');
  btn.innerHTML = text;
}

AD.loadWelcome = function(link, embedded){
    if (typeof(embedded) == 'undefined')
      embedded = 'false';
    var url = AD.template_welcome_uri + "?site=" + AD.site + "&embedded=" + embedded;
    if ($(link).data("img"))
      url = url + "&img=" + $(link).data("img")
    if ($(link).data("img-class"))
      url = url + "&img_class=" + $(link).data("img-class")
    if ($(link).data("img-title"))
      url = url + "&img_title=" + $(link).data("img-title")
    if ($(link).data("img-description"))
      url = url + "&img_description=" + $(link).data("img-description")
    if ($(link).data("title"))
      url = url + "&title=" + $(link).data("title")
    if ($(link).data("redirect-uri"))
      url = url + "&redirect_uri=" + $(link).data("redirect-uri")
    if (AD.enable_signup === false)
      url = url + "&enable_signup=false"

    $.ajax({
      url: url,
      type: "GET",
      success: function (data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
        window.localStorage['welcome_form_'+embedded] = data;
        data = data.replace(/data-origin=\"(\S+)\"/, "data-origin=\"" + document.location.href + "\"");
        if (embedded == 'false') {
          $("#kenneth-modal").html(data);
          $("#kenneth-modal").addClass("blocking-modal show-modal");
          $("body, html").css({"overflow": "hidden"});
        } else {
          $("#kenneth-embedded").html(data);
        }

        if (AD.hasConsent()) {
          // for users who have accepted the consent, we don't show the checkbox on login
          if ($('#js-kth-si-checkbox-accept-terms').length > 0) {
            $('#js-kth-si-checkbox-accept-terms').prop('checked', true);
            $('#js-kth-si-checkbox-accept-terms').hide();
          }
        }

        var signInElement = $('.js-kth-signin'),
            signUpElement = $('.js-kth-signup');

        function setSignInForm() {
          signUpElement.addClass('afd-hide');
          signInElement.removeClass('afd-hide');
          $('.js-kth-tab-signin').addClass('kth-tabs__item--active');
          $('.js-kth-tab-signup').removeClass('kth-tabs__item--active')
        }
        function setSignUpForm() {
          signUpElement.removeClass('afd-hide');
          signInElement.addClass('afd-hide');
          $('.js-kth-tab-signin').removeClass('kth-tabs__item--active');
          $('.js-kth-tab-signup').addClass('kth-tabs__item--active')
        }

        // If signup is not enabled, show only sign in modal
        if (AD.enable_signup === false) {
          setSignInForm();
        }
        // If click in a signin link show modal with signin form visible
        if ($(link).data('modal') == 'signin') {
          setSignInForm()
        }

        // Change form clicking links that do this
        if ($('.js-kth-set-signup').length > 0) {
          $('.js-kth-set-signup').click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            setSignUpForm();
          });
        }
        if ($('.js-kth-set-signin').length > 0) {
          $('.js-kth-set-signin').click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            setSignInForm();
          });
        }

        // Form validations
        function validSignupForm() {
          var email           = document.getElementById('new_user_email'),
              pass            = document.getElementById('new_user_password'),
              name            = document.getElementById('new_user_full_name'),
              btn             = document.getElementById('signup_btn'),
              hintName        = document.getElementById('js-hint-su-full_name'),
              hintMail        = document.getElementById('js-hint-su-email'),
              hintPass        = document.getElementById('js-hint-su-pass'),
              validName       = document.getElementById('js-kth-su-val-full_name'),
              validMail       = document.getElementById('js-kth-su-val-email'),
              validPass       = document.getElementById('js-kth-su-val-pass'),
              verifyReCaptcha = setInterval(function(){
                if ( validConditional() ) {
                  activateBtn();
                  clearInterval(verifyReCaptcha);
                }
              }, 1000);

          document.addEventListener('input', function (e) {
            if ( validConditional() ) {
              activateBtn();
            } else {
              btn.classList.add('afd-btn--not-allowed');
              btn.disabled = true;
            }
          });

          $('#js-kth-checkbox-accept-terms').change(function () {
            if (!$(this).is(":checked")) {
              $('#signup_btn').addClass('afd-btn--not-allowed');
              $('#signup_btn').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
            } else {
              if ( name.value.length > 1 && pass.value.length >= 8 && validateEmail(email.value))
                activateBtn();
            }
          });

          // Valid name
          validateName(name, validName, hintName);

          // Valid email value
          validateEmailValue(email, validMail, hintMail, 'signup');

          // Valid password length
          validatePassLength(pass, validPass, hintPass);

          // Active submit btn
          function activateBtn() {
            btn.classList.remove('afd-btn--not-allowed');
            btn.disabled = false;
            loadingOnSubmit(btn, "Creating Account");
          }

          // Validate if conditions are OK
          function validConditional() {
            if ( name.value.length > 1 && pass.value.length >= 8 && validateEmail(email.value) && $("#js-kth-checkbox-accept-terms").is(':checked')) {
              return true;
            } else {
              return false;
            }
          }

        }
        // Execute only if signup is allow
        if (!!document.getElementById('signup_btn')) {
          validSignupForm();
        }

        function validSigninForm() {
          var email = document.getElementById('user_email'),
              pass = document.getElementById('user_password'),
              btn = document.getElementById('signin_btn'),
              hintMail = document.getElementById('js-hint-si-email'),
              hintPass = document.getElementById('js-hint-si-pass'),
              validMail = document.getElementById('js-kth-si-val-email'),
              forgot = document.getElementById('js-kth-forgot');

          document.addEventListener('input', function (e) {
            // Active submit btn
            if (pass.value.length >= 1 && validateEmail(email.value) && $("#js-kth-si-checkbox-accept-terms").is(':checked')) {
              btn.classList.remove('afd-btn--not-allowed');
              btn.disabled = false;
              loadingOnSubmit(btn, "Accessing");
            } else {
              btn.classList.add('afd-btn--not-allowed');
              btn.disabled = true;
            }
          });

          // validate terms and conditions
          $('#js-kth-si-checkbox-accept-terms').change(function () {
            if (!$(this).is(":checked")) {
              btn.classList.add('afd-btn--not-allowed');
              btn.disabled = true;
            } else {
              if (pass.value.length >= 1 && validateEmail(email.value) && $("#js-kth-si-checkbox-accept-terms").is(':checked')) {
                btn.classList.remove('afd-btn--not-allowed');
                btn.disabled = false;
              }
            }
          });

          // Valid email value
          validateEmailValue(email, validMail, hintMail, 'signin');

          // Valid password length
          validatePassLength(pass, false, hintPass, forgot);

          // Allow submit form if chrome autofill form
          setTimeout(function(){
            var sel = document.querySelector('#user_email:-webkit-autofill');
            if (sel != null && sel.value) {
              btn.disabled = false;
              btn.classList.remove('afd-btn--not-allowed');
            }
          }, 500);
        }
        validSigninForm();
        // End validations

        // Autofocus on first input form
        if (AD.enable_signup === true) {
          setTimeout("document.getElementById('new_user_full_name').focus();", 100);
        } else {
          setTimeout("document.getElementById('user_email').focus();", 100);
        }

        AD.modalOpened = true;
      },
      error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
        if (embedded == 'false')
          $("#kenneth-modal").html(textStatus);
        else
          $("kenneth-embedded").html(textStatus);
      }
    });
};

AD.embedWelcome = function (domElement) {
  AD.loadWelcome(domElement,'true');
};

AD.embedInvitation = function(domElement, embedded) {
  var url = AD.template_invite + "?site="+AD.site;
  if ($(domElement).data("img"))
    url = url + "&img=" + $(domElement).data("img")
  if ($(domElement).data("icon"))
    url = url + "&icon=" + $(domElement).data("icon")
  if ($(domElement).data("title"))
    url = url + "&invitation-title=" + $(domElement).data("invitation-title")
  if ($(domElement).data("message"))
    url = url + "&message=" + $(domElement).data("message")
  if ($(domElement).data("cta"))
    url = url + "&cta=" + $(domElement).data("cta")
  if ($(domElement).data("cancel"))
    url = url + "&cancel=" + $(domElement).data("cancel")

  $.ajax({
    url: url,
    type: "GET",
    success: function (data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
      $("#kenneth-modal").html(data);
      $("#kenneth-modal").addClass("show-modal");
      $("#kenneth-modal .js-cta").click(function() {
        AD.openWelcome();
        try {
          ga('send', 'event', 'Kenneth Invite', 'Call to Action', $(this).text());
        } catch(err) {}
      });
      AD.modalOpened = true;
    },
    error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
      $("#kenneth-modal").html(textStatus);
    }
  });
};

AD.openWelcome = function (link) {
  AD.loadWelcome(link);
};

AD.invitationCheck = function (domElement) {
  if(AD.device() != 'desktop' || AD.userLang() == 'cn-zh')
    return true;

  if (AD.hasConsent() && AD.CurrentUser.id === null && !($.cookie('ad_session') || $.cookie('adat'))) {
    setTimeout(function() {
      if (!$.cookie('kenneth_invitation')) {
        if (AD.modalOpened === false) {
          AD.loadWelcome(domElement);
        }

        $.cookie('kenneth_invitation', new Date().toJSON().slice(0,10), {
          expires: 120,
          domain: AD.domain,
          path: '/'
        });
      }
      else if ($.cookie('kenneth_invitation') && !$.cookie('kenneth_invitation_small')) {
        if (AD.modalOpened === false) {
          AD.embedInvitation(domElement);
        }
      }
      AD.invited = true;
    }, 10000);

    $(document).on("click", ".kenneth-modal__dont-invite", function () {
      $.cookie('kenneth_invitation_small', new Date().toJSON().slice(0,10), {
        expires: 45,
        domain: AD.domain,
        path: '/'
      });
      AD.modalOpened = false;
    });
  }
};

AD.forgotPassword = function (link) {
  url = AD.template_forgot_uri + "?site=" + AD.site;
  if (link !== 'undefined') {
    if ($(link).data("title"))
      url = url + "&title=" + $(link).data("title")
    if ($(link).data("redirect-uri"))
      url = url + "&redirect_uri=" + $(link).data("redirect-uri")
  }
  $.ajax({
    url: url,
    type: "GET",
    success: function (data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
      $("#kenneth-modal").html(data);
      $("#kenneth-modal").addClass("blocking-modal show-modal");
      AD.modalOpened = true;

      var email = document.getElementById('user_email'),
          btn = document.getElementById('forgot_btn'),
          hintMail = document.getElementById('js-hint-f-email'),
          validMail = document.getElementById('js-kth-f-val-email');

      document.addEventListener('input', function (e) {
        // Active submit btn
        if (validateEmail(email.value)) {
          btn.classList.remove('afd-btn--not-allowed');
        } else {
          btn.classList.add('afd-btn--not-allowed');
        }
      });
      validateEmailValue(email, validMail, hintMail, 'forgot');
    },
    error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
      $("#kenneth-modal").html(textStatus);
      $("#kenneth-modal").addClass("blocking-modal show-modal");
    }
  });
};

AD.logout = function () {
  $.ajax({
    url: AD.sign_out_uri,
    type: "DELETE",
    success: function () {
      AD.CurrentUser = null;

      if(AD.localStorageAvailable()) {
        window.localStorage.removeItem('kenneth_me_html');
        window.localStorage.removeItem('kenneth_me_html_created_at');
        window.localStorage.removeItem('kth_current_user');
        window.localStorage.removeItem('kth_access_token');
        window.localStorage.removeItem('kenneth_updated_at');
      }

      if (AD.logout_options != null && AD.logout_options.redirect_after != undefined) {
        window.location.href = AD.logout_options.redirect_after;
        return false;
      }

      if (AD.reload_on_logout)
        window.location.reload();
      else
        AD.showUser();
      if (AD.callback != null)
        AD.callback();
    }
  });
  return false;
};

AD.showConfirmationAlert = function() {
  if (AD.CurrentUser.id && !AD.CurrentUser.legacy_confirmed && !AD.CurrentUser.confirmed_at) {
    var newItem = document.createElement("div");
    newItem.innerHTML = '<div class="afd-container-main clearfix">We sent you a validation email to ' + AD.CurrentUser.email + ' with instructions to activate your account.<a href="https://account.archdaily.com/' + AD.site + '/info" target="blank" class="kth-confirm-account-why">Learn more</a><div class="js-open-validation-modal kth-confirm-account-cta">Haven&#39;t received validation email?</div></div>';
    newItem.classList.add('kth-confirm-account-msg');
    var newModal = document.createElement("div");
    newModal.innerHTML = '<div class="afd-modal-wrap afd-modal-wrap__center"><div class="afd-modal-content afd-modal-size40"><div class="afd-modal-header"><div class="js-close-modal kth-close-modal"><button class="close">✕</button></div></div><div class="afd-modal-body afd-modal-body--small"><div class="afd-post-content"><h3>Quick reminder:</h3><ul><li>It can take up to 5 minutes for the email to reach your inbox.</li><li>Did you check your spam? <em>(email subject: Activate your ArchDaily account)</em></li><li>Are you sure you are checking <strong>' + AD.CurrentUser.email + '</strong>?</li></ul><p>If you have done all of this and still can&#39;t find the email</p></div><a href="#send-validation-email" onclick="javascript: AD.resend_confirmation_email();" class="afd-btn afd-btn--full afd-btn--big js-submit-validation">Resend validation email</a></div></div></div>'
    newModal.classList.add('js-validation-email-modal', 'kth-validation-email-modal');
    document.body.insertBefore(newModal, document.body.firstChild);
    document.body.insertBefore(newItem, document.body.firstChild);
  }
};

AD.should_load_menu = function() {
  if (AD.localStorageAvailable()) {
    if (AD.CurrentUser.updated_at) {
      return ''+AD.CurrentUser.updated_at !== ''+localStorage['kenneth_updated_at'];
    } else {
      return true;
    }
  } else
    // if we dont have localStorage, we need to always load the upper menu
    return true;
};

AD.load_upper_menu = function() {
  if (AD.should_load_menu()) {
    // ask for the kenneth me template
    var headers = {};
    var token = AD.getAccessToken();
    if (token !== null)
      headers["Authorization"] = "Bearer " + token;
    $.ajax({
      url: AD.template_me_uri + "?site=" + AD.site,
      type: "GET",
      headers: headers,
      success: function (data) {
        $("#kenneth-root").html(data);
        if($("#kenneth-root-simple").length > 0)
          $("#kenneth-root-simple").html(data.split('<!-- kenneth-dropdown -->')[0]);
        if(AD.localStorageAvailable()) {
          localStorage["kenneth_me_html"] = data;
        }

        $(document).trigger('kenneth:rendered');
      },
      error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
        $("#kenneth-root").html(textStatus);
        if($("#kenneth-root-simple").length > 0)
          $("#kenneth-root-simple").html(textStatus.split('<!-- kenneth-dropdown -->')[0]);

        $(document).trigger('kenneth:rendered');
      }
    });
  } else {
    $("#kenneth-root").html(window.localStorage["kenneth_me_html"]);
    if($("#kenneth-root-simple").length > 0)
      $("#kenneth-root-simple").html(window.localStorage["kenneth_me_html"].split("<!-- kenneth-dropdown -->")[0]);
    $(document).trigger('kenneth:rendered');
  }
};

AD.setCurrentUser = function(data) {
  if (AD.profile_type === 'minimal') {
    AD.CurrentUser = {
      id: data.id,
      email: data.email,
      full_name: data.full_name,
      avatar: data.avatar,
      confirmed_at: data.confirmed_at,
      legacy_confirmed: data.legacy_confirmed,
      updated_at: data.updated_at,
      accepted_at: data.accepted_at
    };
  } else {
    AD.CurrentUser = {
      id: data.id,
      email: data.email,
      full_name: data.full_name,
      about_me: data.about_me,
      avatar: data.avatar,
      country: data.country,
      ocupation: data.ocupation,
      website: data.website,
      facebook: data.facebook,
      twitter: data.twitter,
      instagram: data.instagram,
      pinterest: data.pinterest,
      birth_date: data.birth_date,
      confirmed_at: data.confirmed_at,
      legacy_confirmed: data.legacy_confirmed,
      updated_at: data.updated_at,
      accepted_at: data.accepted_at
    };
  }
};

AD.getUser = function () {
  var headers = {};
  var token = AD.getAccessToken();
  if (token !== null)
    headers["Authorization"] = "Bearer " + token;
  if (token !== null || AD.legacyCompatibility()) {
    // now, we bring the user profile information back
    var url = AD.profile_uri;
    if (AD.profile_type === 'minimal')
      url += '&minimal=true';
    $.ajax({
      url: url,
      type: "POST",
      headers: headers,
      contentType: 'application/json',
      dataType: 'json',
      success: function (data) {
        AD.setCurrentUser(data);
        AD.load_upper_menu();
        if (AD.localStorageAvailable()) {
          localStorage['kenneth_updated_at'] = AD.CurrentUser.updated_at;
        }
        // trigger an event informing other sites, the user has been loaded correctly to AD.CurrentUser
        $(document).trigger('kenneth:successful-login');
      },
      error: function(err) {
        if (err.status === 404) {
          AD.load_upper_menu();
          $(document).trigger('kenneth:anonymous-access');
        }
      }
    });
  } else {
    AD.load_upper_menu();
    $(document).trigger('kenneth:anonymous-access');
  }
};

// response: js Object
AD.showMessage = function (dom_id, response) {
  var obj = $(dom_id);
  var json_response = null;

  obj.empty();

  try {
    if (typeof(JSON.parse(response)) == 'object')
      json_response = JSON.parse(response);
    else
      json_response = response;

    if (json_response.hasOwnProperty('error')) {
      var p = $("<p class='kenneth-validation'>").html(json_response.error);
      obj.html(p);
    }
    else if (json_response.hasOwnProperty('errors')) {
      var ul = $("<ul class='kenneth-validation'>");
      $.each(json_response.errors, function (k, val) {
        var li = $("<li class='kenneth-validation__item'><strong>" + (k.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + k.slice(1)).replace(/_/, '') + "</strong> " + val + "</li>");
        ul.append(li);
      });
      obj.html(ul);
    }
    else{
      obj.addClass('kenneth-modal__success');
      obj.html(json_response);
    }
  }
  catch(err) {
    obj.addClass('kenneth-modal__error');
    obj.html(response);
  }
};

AD.afterLogin = function(data) {
  AD.setCurrentUser(data.resource);

  if (!AD.use_cookie && AD.localStorageAvailable()) {
    window.localStorage['kth_access_token'] = data.access_token;
  }

  // if the user specified some redirect uri on the form, we redirect to that location
  if (AD.redirect_uri != null) {
    window.location.href = AD.redirect_uri;
    return false;
  }

  if (AD.reload_on_login)
    window.location.reload();
  else {
    $("#kenneth-modal").removeClass("blocking-modal show-modal");
    $("body, html").css({"overflow":"visible"});
    if (AD.callback != null)
      AD.callback();
  }
  AD.modalOpened = false;
};

AD.resend_confirmation_email = function() {
  if (AD.CurrentUser != undefined && AD.CurrentUser.id != undefined) {
    $.ajax({
      url: AD.resend_confirmation_email_uri,
      type: "POST",
      data: JSON.stringify({ 'email': AD.CurrentUser.email }),
      contentType: 'application/json',
      dataType: 'json',
      success: function (data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
        AD.create_modal_content(data.message);
      },
      error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
        AD.create_modal_content(jqXHR.responseJSON.message);
      }
    });
  }
};

AD.check_user_email = function(email, hint, validMail) {
  $.ajax({
    url: AD.check_uri,
    type: "POST",
    data: { 'email': email },
    dataType: 'json',
    error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
      hint.innerHTML = jqXHR.responseJSON.message;
      hint.classList.remove('afd-hide');
      validMail.classList.remove('kth-input-val--true');
      validMail.classList.add('kth-input-val--false');
    }
  });
};

AD.create_modal_content = function(content) {
  var modal = '<div class="kenneth-modal kenneth-modal__bg-black kenneth-modal__center-wrap"><div id="kenneth-modal-content"><div class="kth-modal__close">';
      modal += '<a class="kth-modal__close__icon" href="#" rel="kenneth-close-modal">&#10006;</a></div><div class="kenneth-modal__container">';
      modal += content;
      modal += '</div></div></div>';
  $("#kenneth-modal").html(modal);
  $("#kenneth-modal").addClass("blocking-modal show-modal");
  $("body, html").css({"overflow": "hidden"});
};

AD.deleteAccount = function () {
  var options = arguments;
  $.ajax({
    url: AD.delete_uri,
    type: "POST",
    headers: { "Authorization": "Bearer " + AD.getAccessToken() },
    dataType: 'json',
    success: function (data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
      if (jqXHR.status == 204) {
        window.location.replace(AD.goodbye_uri + "&name="+AD.CurrentUser.full_name);
      } else {
        if (typeof options[0] === 'object' && typeof options[0].responseError === 'function') {
          options[0].responseError.call(data, textStatus, jqXHR);
        }
      }
    },
    error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
      if (typeof options[0] === 'object' && typeof options[0].serverError === 'function') {
        options[0].serverError.call(jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown);
      }
    }
  });
};

AD.isReady = function () {
  // initialize the SDK if the user didn't call the init method
  if (!AD.initialized) {
    AD.init();
  }

  // add event after the user has been loaded
  $(document).on('kenneth:successful-login', function(e) {
    AD.showConfirmationAlert();
  });

  // add event after we check the access has been anonymous
  $(document).on('kenneth:anonymous-access', function(e) {
    if($('#kenneth-embedded').length > 0)
      AD.embedWelcome($('#kenneth-embedded'));

    if($("#kenneth-invitation").length > 0)
      AD.invitationCheck($("#kenneth-invitation"));
  });

  $(document).on('kenneth:rendered', function(e) {
    AD.checkConsent();
  });

  AD.cleanStorage();
  AD.getUser();

  if(AD.auto_open && AD.hasConsent())
    AD.openWelcome();

  // submits form.forgot (forgot your password)
  $(document).on("submit", "form.forgot", function () {
    var obj       = $(this);
    var form_data = obj.serializeArray();
    var url       = AD.prepend_api + obj.attr("action") + "?site="+AD.site;
    $.ajax({
      url: url,
      type: "POST",
      data: JSON.stringify({ 'email': form_data[0]['value'] }),
      contentType: 'application/json',
      dataType: 'json',
      success: function (data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
        if (jqXHR.status == 200) {
          //AD.openWelcome();
          AD.showMessage(".forgot .messages", data.message);
          document.querySelector('.messages').classList.remove('kenneth-modal__error');
          var removibleItems = document.querySelectorAll('.js-kth-forgot-1');
          for (var i = 0; i < removibleItems.length; i++) {
            removibleItems[i].classList.add('afd-hide');
          }
        }
      },
      error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
        if (jqXHR.status == 404 || jqXHR.status == 400)  {
          AD.showMessage(".forgot .messages", jqXHR.responseJSON.message);
        }
      }
    });
    return false;
  });

  $(document).on("submit", "form.register-form", function() {
    var obj       = $(this);
    var form_data = obj.serializeArray();

    //if (AD.domain.includes("kenneth")) // hack for csrf validation inside own kenneth
      //  $("meta[name='csrf-token']").attr("content", $('.register-form-csrf-token').val());
    $.ajax({
      url: AD.sign_up_uri+ "?site=" + AD.site,
      type: "POST",
      data: JSON.stringify({ 'email': form_data[1]['value'], 'full_name': form_data[0]['value'], 'password': form_data[2]['value'] }),
      contentType: 'application/json',
      dataType: 'json',
      success: function (data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
        AD.afterLogin(data);
        return false;
      },
      error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
        if (jqXHR.status == 400) {
          var hintMail    = document.getElementById('js-hint-su-email'),
            validMail     = document.getElementById('js-kth-su-val-email'),
            hintFullName  = document.getElementById('js-hint-su-full_name'),
            validFullName = document.getElementById('js-kth-su-val-full_name'),
            validPass     = document.getElementById('js-kth-su-val-pass'),
            btn           = document.getElementById('signup_btn'),
            hintPass      = document.getElementById('js-hint-su-pass');
          var data        = JSON.parse(jqXHR.responseText);

          removeLoadingOnSubmit(btn, "Create Account");

          for (var key in data['errors'][0]) {
            if (data['errors'][0].hasOwnProperty(key)) {
              if (key == 'email') {
                validMail.classList.add('kth-input-val--false');
                validMail.classList.remove('kth-input-val--true');
                hintMail.classList.remove('afd-hide');
                hintMail.innerHTML = data['errors'][0]['email'];
              } else if (key == 'password') {
                validPass.classList.add('kth-input-val--false');
                validPass.classList.remove('kth-input-val--true');
                hintPass.classList.remove('afd-hide');
                hintPass.innerText = data['errors'][0]['password'];
              } else if (key == 'full_name') {
                validFullName.classList.add('kth-input-val--false');
                validFullName.classList.remove('kth-input-val--true');
                hintFullName.classList.remove('afd-hide');
                hintFullName.innerText = data['errors'][0]['full_name'];
              }
            }
          }
          hint = true;
        }
        else if (jqXHR.status == 422)
          AD.showMessage(".js-kth-signup .messages", parse_errors(jqXHR.responseText));
      }
    });
    return false;
  });

  // submits form.welcome (sign in and sign out)
  $(document).on("submit", "form.login-form", function () {
    var obj          = $(this);
    var form_data    = obj.serializeArray();

    $.ajax({
      url: AD.sign_in_uri + "?site="+AD.site,
      type: "POST",
      data: JSON.stringify({ 'email': form_data[0]['value'], 'password': form_data[1]['value'] }),
      contentType: 'application/json',
      dataType: 'json',
      success: function (data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
        return AD.afterLogin(data);
      },
      error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
        // we can receive two responses from the backend. A 400 error is some error in the login
        // process (wrong password, validation error, etc.). A 404 error is when the user (email)
        // doesn't exists in the database.
        var btn = document.getElementById('signin_btn');
        removeLoadingOnSubmit(btn, "Log in");
        if (jqXHR.status == 400)
          AD.showMessage(".js-kth-signin .messages", parse_errors(jqXHR.responseText));
        else if (jqXHR.status == 404)
          AD.showMessage(".js-kth-signin .messages", "This email doesn’t have an account on ArchDaily. Maybe you want to create a new account");
      }
    });

    return false;
  });

  // lost your password
  $(document).on("click", "a[rel='kenneth-forgot']", function () {
    AD.forgotPassword(this);
    return false;
  });

  // click to login
  $(document).on("click", "a[rel='kenneth-open-modal']", function () {
    AD.openWelcome(this);
    return false;
  });

  // click to logout
  $(document).on("click", "a[rel='kenneth-logout']", function () {
    AD.logout();
    return false;
  });

  // click to close modal
  $(document).on("click", "a[rel='kenneth-close-modal']", function () {
    $("#kenneth-modal").removeClass("blocking-modal show-modal");
    $("body, html").css({"overflow":"visible"});
    AD.modalOpened = false;
    if(AD.invited){
      try {
        if($(this).data("origin") == "invitation")
          ga('send', 'event', 'Kenneth Invite', 'Close', 'First step (' + $(this).text() + ')');
        else
          ga('send', 'event', 'Kenneth Invite', 'Close', 'Second step (' + $(this).text() + ')');
      } catch(err) {}

      AD.invited = false;
    }
    return false;
  });

  $(document).on("click", "span.fb-login a", function () {
    var obj = $(this);

    window.location.href = obj.data("href") + '?site=' + AD.site;
    AD.modalOpened = false;
    return false;
  });

  $(document).on("click", ".js-open-validation-modal", function() {
    $(".js-validation-email-modal").addClass("kth-validation-email-modal__show");
  });

  $(document).on("click", ".js-close-modal", function() {
    $(".js-validation-email-modal").removeClass("kth-validation-email-modal__show");
  });

  $(document).on("click", ".js-submit-validation", function() {
    $(".js-validation-email-modal").removeClass("kth-validation-email-modal__show");
  });

  $(document).on("click", ".js-account-unsubscribe", function () {
    AD.deleteAccount();
  });

  if (AD.callback != null)
    AD.callback();
};

AD.checkConsent = function() {
  if (! AD.hasConsent()) {
    AD.showConsentBanner();
  } else {
    AD.removeConsentElements();
  }
}

AD.hasConsent = function() {
  if (AD.CurrentUser.accepted_at) {
    return true;
  }

  var date = new Date($.cookie('ad-consented_at'));

  return ! isNaN(date.getTime());
}

AD.setConsentCookie = function() {
  $.cookie('ad-consented_at', new Date().toISOString(), {
    path: '/',
    domain: AD.domain,
    expires: 5 * 365
  });
}

AD.acceptConsent = function() {
  if (AD.CurrentUser.id) {
    // we have a signed in user, we need to persist the consent
    $('#gdpr-consent').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
    $.ajax({
      url: AD.accept_terms_uri,
      type: "POST",
      headers: { "Authorization": "Bearer " + AD.getAccessToken() },
      dataType: 'json',
      success: function (data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
        if (jqXHR.status == 200) {
          AD.CurrentUser.accepted_at = data.accepted_at;
          AD.hideConsentBanner();
          // we also create the cookie in this case
          AD.setConsentCookie();
        } else {
          console.log("[ERROR-" + jqXHR.status + "] " + data);
          $('#gdpr-consent').attr('disabled', null);
        }
      },
      error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
        console.log("[ERROR-" + jqXHR.status + "] " + errorThrown)
        $('#gdpr-consent').attr('disabled', null);
      }
    });
  } else {
    // anonymous case
    AD.setConsentCookie();

    if (typeof arguments[0] === 'object' && typeof arguments[0].callback === 'function') {
      arguments[0].callback.call();
    }
  }
}

AD.showConsentBanner = function() {
  var $toast = $('<div class="kth-toast kth-toast--bottom"></div>');
  var $container = $('<div class="afd-container-main"></div>');
  var $body = $('<div class="kth-toast__body"></div>');
  var $action = $('<div class="kth-toast__action"></div>');
  var $button = $('<button id="gdpr-consent" class="afd-btn afd-btn--big"></button>');
  var $heading = $('<h3 class="afd-title--small"></h3>');
  var $copy = $('<p></p>');

  $heading.html('By using ArchDaily, you agree to our <a href="https://www.archdaily.com/terms-of-use/">Terms of Use</a>, <a href="https://www.archdaily.com/legal/">Privacy Policy</a> and <a href="http://www.archdaily.com/content/cookie-policy">Cookie Policy</a>.');
  $copy.html('If you want to make the best of your experience on our site, <a href="https://my.archdaily.com/">sign-up</a>.');
  $button.text('I accept');

  $action.append($button);
  $body.append($heading).append($copy);
  $container.append($body).append($action);
  $toast.append($container);

  $('body').append($toast);

  $(document).on('click', '#gdpr-consent', function() {
    AD.acceptConsent({
      callback: AD.hideConsentBanner
    });
  });

  $($toast)
    .hide()
    .fadeIn();
}

AD.hideConsentBanner = function () {
  $('.kth-toast').fadeOut(function() {
    AD.removeConsentElements();
    AD.invitationCheck();
  });
}

AD.removeConsentElements = function () {
  $('.kth-toast').remove();
}

   var googletag = googletag || {};
  googletag.cmd = googletag.cmd || [];

  (function() {
    var gads = document.createElement('script');
    gads.async = true;
    gads.type = 'text/javascript';
    var useSSL = 'https:' == document.location.protocol;
    gads.src = (useSSL ? 'https:' : 'http:') + '//www.googletagservices.com/tag/js/gpt.js';
    var node = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
    node.parentNode.insertBefore(gads, node);
  })();

  googletag.cmd.push(function() {
    $('.js-slot').each(function() {
      var slotDevices = this.dataset.device.split(";");
      var slotIndex = slotDevices.indexOf(device);
      if ( slotIndex < 0 )
        return true;
      var slotSize = this.dataset.slotSize.split(";")[slotIndex];
      googletag.defineSlot('/1021178/' + this.dataset.slotName, eval(slotSize), this.id).addService(googletag.pubads());
    });
    googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
    googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs();
    googletag.enableServices();
  });

  googletag.cmd.push(function() {
    $('.js-slot').each(function() {
      var slotDevices = this.dataset.device.split(";");
      var slotIndex = slotDevices.indexOf(device);
      if ( slotIndex < 0 )
        return true;
      googletag.display(this.id);
    });
  });
